--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Table CUSTOMERS
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE TABLE "CUSTOMERS" 
   (	"CUSTOMER_ID" NUMBER(*,0), 
	"EMAIL_ADDRESS" VARCHAR2(255 CHAR), 
	"FULL_NAME" VARCHAR2(255 CHAR)
   ) ;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Table ORDERS
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE TABLE "ORDERS" 
   (	"ORDER_ID" NUMBER(*,0), 
	"ORDER_DATETIME" TIMESTAMP (6), 
	"CUSTOMER_ID" NUMBER(*,0), 
	"ORDER_STATUS" VARCHAR2(10 CHAR), 
	"STORE_ID" NUMBER(*,0)
   ) ;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Table ORDER_ITEMS
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE TABLE "ORDER_ITEMS" 
   (	"ORDER_ID" NUMBER(*,0), 
	"LINE_ITEM_ID" NUMBER(*,0), 
	"PRODUCT_ID" NUMBER(*,0), 
	"UNIT_PRICE" NUMBER(10,2), 
	"QUANTITY" NUMBER(*,0)
   ) ;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Table PRODUCTS
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE TABLE "PRODUCTS" 
   (	"PRODUCT_ID" NUMBER, 
	"PRODUCT_NAME" VARCHAR2(255 CHAR), 
	"UNIT_PRICE" NUMBER(10,2), 
	"PRODUCT_DETAILS" BLOB, 
	"PRODUCT_IMAGE" BLOB, 
	"IMAGE_MIME_TYPE" VARCHAR2(512 CHAR), 
	"IMAGE_FILENAME" VARCHAR2(512 CHAR), 
	"IMAGE_CHARSET" VARCHAR2(512 CHAR), 
	"IMAGE_LAST_UPDATED" DATE
   ) ;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Table STORES
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE TABLE "STORES" 
   (	"STORE_ID" NUMBER(*,0), 
	"STORE_NAME" VARCHAR2(255 CHAR), 
	"WEB_ADDRESS" VARCHAR2(100 CHAR), 
	"PHYSICAL_ADDRESS" VARCHAR2(512 CHAR), 
	"LATITUDE" NUMBER, 
	"LONGITUDE" NUMBER, 
	"LOGO_MIME_TYPE" VARCHAR2(512 CHAR), 
	"LOGO_FILENAME" VARCHAR2(512 CHAR), 
	"LOGO_CHARSET" VARCHAR2(512 CHAR), 
	"LOGO_LAST_UPDATED" DATE, 
	"LOGO" BLOB
   ) ;

--  DDL for Trigger CUSTOMER_SEQ_TRG
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE EDITIONABLE TRIGGER "CUSTOMER_SEQ_TRG" BEFORE
    INSERT ON customers
    FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
    SELECT
        customer_seq.NEXTVAL
    INTO :new.customer_id
    FROM
        dual;
END;

/
ALTER TRIGGER "CUSTOMER_SEQ_TRG" ENABLE;
